< text>
If I could give this place less than one star, I would. If Google reviews had black holes for bad reviews, I would push this place past the event horizon.

Do not shop at this rip-off establishment.

A few days ago my girlfriend and I bought two iPhones there at an OK price. The salesperson sold us cases and screen protectors for the phones. We did not ask the prices for those, but I am willing to pay more than the Amazon price to support a local business. They also sold us one pair of earbuds. We did not know that the regular iPhone earbuds were in the boxes with the phones. The salesperson said the earbuds were regularly $120, but we would get them for $70.

When we got home we found out that we had been charged $119.96 for the cases and covers, that we did not need extra earbuds, that the earbuds we had bought should retail for about $30, and that the most expensive iPhone 11 screen protectors on Amazon are $20 for a two-pack. The packaging for the screen protectors was not in the bag with the iPhone boxes, earbuds and receipts.

When we returned to the store today, the salesperson told us he had done everything correctly, that $29.99 each was the correct price for the screen protectors and cases, and that the earbuds were not returnable, even though the package had not been opened. When I asked to speak to the manager, the salesperson claimed to be the manager and owner of the store. Another Cricket store told us later that they sell an iPhone 11 screen protector for $14.99. I am going to guess that price is for a two-pack.

I got no help from Cricket phone and chat support. They told me to return to the store and ask for the manager. They could not give me the name of the store owner, nor could they verify that the salesperson's name on the purchase receipt matched the name of the owner.

One can accept the $30 price for each case and add another $30 for screen protectors (rather high prices, but legitimate). That comes to $90 that we should have been charged. The total charge for the earbuds we don't want, the cases, and the protectors was $190. This store ripped us off for $100.

Let me repeat. This store overcharged us by $100 and refused to make it right.

Rip-off establishment. Do not shop there!</text>

<Rate>1< /Rate><Text>I found out about this hair salon through a recommendation from someone in a Facebook group. Because of that, I wanted to try it out. Also because it was very closeby, and the prices were really good. Now, a week after I got my haircut, I am still bothered by the experience I had here.

First, it was very hard to communicate with the lady who was cutting my hair because she didn't speak English very well.

Second, while she was combing through my hair, she caught and pulled my earring which was just a small flat stud earring. And it wasn't until after I came home that I noticed that it was bleeding and it got irritated.

Now the third and the deal breaker. Upon paying, the lady charged me $25. So I asked her how it got to that amount. The reason why I got surprised by this and asked her is because on their Facebook page (under the tab "services"), it clearly says "specialty women's haircuts - $15". And the picture shown in that category is even the same length/style as the cut I got! So, why am I being charged $10 more? So here's what really got me and really turned me off. As I was showing her what it says on their Facebook page, her demeanor changed and she just suddenly rushed and told me "ok, just give me $20". I kept going back and forth with her showing her what's on this page and asking her why she was charging me more. The way she was acting about it just did NOT feel right. I attended Movies in the Park last night for the kickoff of its 13th season of free family movies and free hotdogs.  It's held Every Saturday in August and is definitely a community favorite.

<text>I was in a bind to trying to find a few parts, oils, and accessories for a few of my motorcycles for an upcoming trip. I had tried calling around to multiple places and no one seemed to be able to help, until I called Advanced Motorsports! I called, and left a message within five minutes I got a voicemail back from the owners asking what parts and accessories I was looking for, I responded back with my list and and told me that they will call me back in 30 minutes. About 15 minutes later I was surprised and relieved that Juanita was able to order my parts overnight them and have them ready for me for pick up the very next day! The process is extremely easy and convenient using text messages, phone calls and voice recorded messages to communicate effectively and promptly (with a lot of detail might I add). Not only were they able to overnight the parts they were able to find and procure some parts that were really hard to find ; some places estimating close to 2 to 3 weeks!! not with Advanced Motorsports. This is a one stop shop, anything you need from Carb rebuild kits, desert flag whips, Whip mounts, light up whips, heck they even offered to try and find me some riding gear to get to me in time in order for me to save myself from running around the city trying to find helmets and boots. This is been my third experience working with advanced motorsports and I must say German and Juanita are amazing and true masters of their craft. Environment: Clean, very very clean. The corners near where the couch is and the bathroom are basically spotless.

< review>
Ok! I went to this Trader Joe's for the first time. I was in my nursing apparel and had my badge in hand. I simply wanted to stop by and grab a few items after working a long depressing shift. I presented my badge to the gentleman at the door and he tells me that they are no longer allowing essential workers to enter the store and we are to wait as well. Now I normally shop at the Trader Joe's in Fremont but I relocated to Oakland. Now Healthcare workers don't ask for much and I literally ook that as a Slap in the face. I know that ever RN and physician is incredibly pressed for time because we are all working extremely long, exhausting, and chaotic hours. Now you mean to tell me when we get off we have to stand in line 20 - 30 min. before we can go into a store to make some much needed grocery. I declare this was the 1st and last time that I will ever shop at this Trader Joe's. If I was not so tired and depressed about all the patients that I see dying from CVD everyday, I would have left this store without shopping at all. Plus I just wanted to grab a few things to take to work so that I could have something to eat. This World Truly Have Issues especially when you take a simple gesture and discard during such chaotic times!!!<//review>

< Review>
A fairly decent sized store that isn't all over packed and tight to navigate thru like some other locations are. The crew is always pleasant. They also offer samples everyday of one or more of their products, which can be a helpful way to find something new you'll like that you couldn't afford to take a chance on buying. Personally, I also love that they help keep our local food bank stocked with all kinds of different items. I am also a client and lucky enough to benefit from their offerings, however, I find their pricing to be quite competitive overall but when it comes to the staples like milk, butter and eggs its hard to find a better deal than Trader Joe's everyday prices.< /Review>

Favorite place to go for groceries!

Parking: Shares a parking lot with the other stores at the Alameda Shore Center.

Prices: It's not a dollar store, but I think they are pretty decent and worth it. It's definitely cheaper than Whole Foods if that helps you get a better idea of the prices they offer.

<date>1557014814242<//date><rate>4</rate>< text>
OMG, this is my local Trader Joe's, which I visit on average five times a week, and somehow I've never reviewed it? How's that possible? Argh!

Trader Joe's store #109 is located in the middle of the South Shore Shopping Center. There's hundreds of parking spots immediately out front. Conveniently located near the corner of Park Street and Otis Drive, this is the to-go spot for dozens of staples, some keto-friendly foods (including grilled artichoke hearts, cheeses, eggs, hamburger, pork tenderloin, turkey breast, and sopressata salami), and the many TJ-specific offerings (including truffle p√¢te, many really good coffee beans, and seasonal surprises like unsweetened bakers chocolate, cakes and cookies, and mystery bags).

The non-food items, like greeting cards, plants and flowers, and a wide selection of beer, wine, and hard liquors round out any shopping trip.

The staff are absolutely wonderful, know their stock and where they may be found, and are always ready to help you find a TJ treasure. I'm very proud of my local store and hope you come on over to share in the joy.< /text>

<Text>Our go-to store. We come here weekly, because they have a good selection of veggies, fruits, meats, cheeses, snacks, beers and wines. Not to mention the staff is really friendly and the store is well kept (compared to Safeway next door where things are all over the place).

It's not pricey and it's convenient since you have a big parking place and many other stores around (in case you can't get everything here). Sometimes they don't have certain things cause they are changing the labels or getting in something new from someone else, but if you ask they might find something in the back or just tell you the date when they're getting it back on their shelves.

The only downside is that perishable things tend to go bad before their expiration date (salads and fruit I'm looking at you) and we do put them in the fridge and take all the necessary precautions.

The lines are not too long because the staff makes sure there's a sufficient number of check-outs open (again compared to Safeway where you have two registers and 20 people). But if you want to avoid the place being too crowded come in right after they open.

I don't care much for the samples they have, but I was told they are also good.

Would highly recommend you to come here instead of going into Safeway next door.<//Text>< name>
Lea S</name>

Trader Joe's store #109 is located in the middle of the South Shore Shopping Center. There's hundreds of parking spots immediately out front. Conveniently located near the corner of Park Street and Otis Drive, this is the to-go spot for dozens of staples, some keto-friendly foods (including grilled artichoke hearts, cheeses, eggs, hamburger, pork tenderloin, turkey breast, and sopressata salami), and the many TJ-specific offerings (including truffle p√¢te, many really good coffee beans, and seasonal surprises like unsweetened bakers chocolate, cakes and cookies, and mystery bags).

The non-food items, like greeting cards, plants and flowers, and a wide selection of beer, wine, and hard liquors round out any shopping trip.

The staff are absolutely wonderful, know their stock and where they may be found, and are always ready to help you find a TJ treasure. I'm very proud of my local store and hope you come on over to share in the joy.</text>
